MATHEMATICAL LITERACY P2  
MARKING GUID ELINES  
 
MARKS:              100  
  
Symbol  Explanation  
M Method  
MA Method with accuracy  
CA Consistent accuracy  
A Accuracy  
C Conversion  
S Simplification  
RT Reading from a table/graph/ diagram  
SF Correct s ubstitution in a formula  
O Opinion/Explanation/Reasoning  
P Penalty, e.g. for no units, incorrect rounding off , etc.  
R Rounding Off/Reason  
NPR  No penalty for correct rounding minimum two decimal places  
AO Answer only  
MCA  Method with consistent accuracy  
RCA  Rounding with consistent accuracy

MARKING GUIDELINES  
NOTE:  
вАҐ If a candidate answers a question TWICE, only mark the FIRST attempt.  
  
вАҐ If a candidate has crossed out (cancelled) an attempt to a question and NOT redone the 
solution, mark the crossed out (cancelled) version.  
  
вАҐ Consistent Accuracy (CA) applies in ALL aspects of the marking guidelines; however, it 
stops at the second calculation error.  
  
вАҐ If the candidate presents any extra solution when reading from a graph, table, layout plan and 
map, then penalize  for every extra incorrect item presented.

NATIONAL  
SENIOR CERTIFICATE  
 
 GRADE 11   
 
NOVEMBER 202 5 
 
MATHEMATICAL LITERACY P1  
MARKING GUIDELINE  
 
MARKS:  100 
  
 
 This marking guideline  consists of 8 pages.   
  
This document was downloaded from www.ecexams.co.za.

2 MATHEMATICAL LITERACY P1  (EC/ NOV EMBER 2025)  
Copyright reserved   Please turn over   
Symbol  Explanation   
M  Method   
MA  Method with accuracy  
CA  Consistent accuracy  
A  Accuracy  
C  Conversion  
S  Simplification  
RT  Reading from a table/a graph/document/diagram  
SF  Correct substitution in a formula  
O  Opinion/Explanation   
P  Penalty, e.g. for no units, incorrect rounding off, etc.  
R  Rounding off  
NPR  No penalty for correct rounding minimum two decimal places  
AO  Answer only   
MCA  Method with constant accuracy   
   
NOTE:  
вАҐ If a candidate answers a question TWICE, only mark the FIRST attempt.  
вАҐ If a candidate has crossed out an attempt of a question and not redone the question, mark 
the crossed out version.  
вАҐ Consistent accuracy applies in ALL aspects of the marking guideline. Stop marking at the 
second calculation error.  
вАҐ NOTE : Consistent accuracy (CA) does NOT apply in cases of a breakdown.  
вАҐ If the candidate presents any extra solution when reading from a graph and table , then 
penalise for every extra item presented.  
вАҐ As a general marking principle, if a candidate has incurred one mistake and there is 
evidence of sound Mathematics thereafter, then that candidate should lose ONE mark only.  
Topics: F вАУ Finance,  DH вАУ Data Handling,  P вАУ Probability

MA Method with accuracy/ Metode met akkuraatheid  
CA Consistent accuracy/ Volgehoue akkuraatheid

C Conversion/ Herleiding  
S Simplification/ Vereenvoudiging  
RT Reading from table/a graph/document/diagram/ Lees vanaf 
tabel/grafiek/ document/ diagram  
SF Correct substitution in a formula /Korrekte vervanging in formule

eenhede/verkeerde afronding, ens.

NPR  No penalty for correct rounding/ Geen penalisasie vir korrekte afronding nie

MCA  Method with constant accuracy/ Metode met volgehoue akkuraatheid  
RCA  Rounding consistent with accuracy/ Afronding met volgehoue akkuraatheid

Mathematical Literacy/P1/ Wiskundige Geletterdhei d/V1    2           NW/June 2024 /Junie 2024  
Grade 11 вАУ Marking Guidelines/ Nasienriglyne  
 
 
Copyright reserved/Kopiereg voorbehou   Please turn over/Blaai om asseblief  NOTE:  
 
вАҐ If a candidate answers a question TWICE, only mark the FIRST attempt.  
вАҐ If a candidate has crossed out (cancelled) an attempt to a question and NOT redone the 
solution, mark the crossed out (cancelled) version.  
вАҐ Consistent accuracy (CA) applies in ALL aspects of the marking guidelines; however, it 
stops at the second calculation error.  
вАҐ NOTE: consistent accuracy (CA) does not apply in cases of a breakdown.  
вАҐ If the candidate presents any extra solution when reading from a graph, table, layout plan 
and map, then penalise for every extra item presented.  
вАҐ As a general principle, if a candidate has incurred one mistake and there is evidence of 
sound mathematics thereafter, then that candidate should lose one mark only.  
вАҐ Rounding is an independent mark.  
вАҐ In order to award the verification/conclusion mark the candidate must have scored at least 
one mark in the calculation preceding the final conclusion.  
 
 
LET WEL:  
 
вАҐ As вАШn kandidaat вАШn vraag TWEE KEER beantwoord, sien slegs die EERSTE poging na.  
вАҐ As вАШn kandidaat вАШn antwoord van вАШn vraag doodtrek (kanselleer) en nie oordoen nie, sien 
die doodgetrekte (gekanselleerde) poging na.  
вАҐ Volgehoue akkuraatheid (CA) word in ALLE aspekte van die nasienriglyne toegepas, dit 
hou op by die tweede berekeningsfout.  
вАҐ LET WEL : volgehoue akkuraathe id (CA) geld nie  in die geval van вАШn afbreuk nie.  
вАҐ Wanneer вАШn kandidaat aflesings vanaf вАШn grafiek, tabel, uitlegplan en kaart geneem en 
ekstra antwoorde gee, penaliseer vir elke ekstra item.  
вАҐ вАШn Algemene nasienbeginsel is dat indien вАШn kandidaat een fout maak en daarna voortgaan 
met korrekte wiskunde, dat die kandidaat slegs een punt verloor.  
вАҐ Afronding tel as вАШn afsonderlike punt.  
вАҐ Ten einde die verifikasie/gevolgtrekking punt toe te ken moes die kandidaat ten minste 
een punt gekry het in die berekeninge wat lei tot die finale gevolgtrekking.

Mathematical Literacy/P2 /Wiskundige Geletterdheid/V 2 2  NW/November 2024  
Grade/ Graad 11  вАУ Marking Guideline s/Nasienriglyne  
 
 
Copyright reserved /Kopiereg voorbehou   Please turn over/ Blaai om asseblief  NOTE:  
пВЈ If a candidate answers a question TWICE, only mark  the FIRST attempt.  
пВЈ If a candidate has crossed out (cancelled) an attempt to a question and NOT redone the solution, 
mark the crossed out (cancelled) version.  
пВЈ Consistent accuracy (CA) applies in ALL aspects of the marking guidelines; however, it stops 
at the second calculation error.  
пВЈ NOTE:  consistent accuracy (CA) does not apply in cases of a breakdown.  
пВЈ If the candidate presents any extra solution when reading from a graph, table , layout plan and 
map, then penalize  for every extra item presented.  
пВЈ As a general marking principle, if a candidate has incurred one mistake and there is evidence 
of sound mathematics thereafter, then that candidate should lose one mark only.  
пВЈ Rounding is an independent mark.  
пВЈ In opinion type questions marks will only be awarded i f relevant calc ulations are shown.  
 
LET WEL:  
пВЈ As вАШn kandidaat вАШn vraag TWEE KEER beantwoord, sien slegs die EERSTE poging na.  
пВЈ As вАШn kandidaat вАШn antwoord van вАШn vraag doodtrek (kanselleer) en nie oordoen nie, sien die doodgetrekte 
(gekanselleerde) poging na. 
пВЈ Volgehoue akkuraatheid (CA) word in ALLE aspekte van die nasienriglyne toegepas, dit hou op by die 
tweede berekeningsfout.  
пВЈ LET WEL: volgehoue akkuraatheid (CA) geld nie in die geval van вАШn afbreuk nie.  
пВЈ Wanneer вАШn kandidaat aflesings vanaf вАШn grafiek, t abel, uitlegplan en kaart geneem en ekstra antwoorde 
gee, penaliseer vir elke ekstra item.  
пВЈ вАШn Algemene nasienbeginsel is dat indien вАШn kandidaat een fout maak en daarna voortgaan met korrekte 
wiskunde, dat die kandidaat slegs een punt verloor.  
пВЈ Afronding te l as вАШn afsonderlike punt.  
пВЈ Ten einde die verifikasie/gevolgtrekking punt toe te ken moes die kandidaat ten minste een punt gekry 
het in die berekeninge wat lei tot die finale gevolgtrekking.

it stops at the second calculation error.  
вАҐ If the candidate presents any extra solution when reading from a graph, table, layout 
plan and map, then penalise for every extra incorrect item presented.

2 MATHEMATICAL LITERACY P2  (EC/ NOVEMBER  2023) 
Copyright reserved   Please turn over   
MARKING GUIDELINES  
 
NOTE:  
 
вАҐ If a candidate answers a question TWICE, only mark the FIRST attempt.  
 
вАҐ If a candidate has crossed out (cancelled) an attempt to a question and NOT redone the 
solution, mark the crossed out (cancelled version) . 
 
вАҐ Consistent Accuracy (CA) applies in ALL aspects of the marking gui delines; however, it 
stops at the second calculation error.  
 
вАҐ If the candidate presents any extra solution when reading from a graph, table, layout plan and 
map, then penalise for every extra incorrect item presented.  
 
LET WEL:  
 
вАҐ As ≈Й kandidaat ≈Й vraag TWEE keer beantwoord merk slegs die EERSTE poging.  
 
вАҐ As ≈Й kandidaat ≈Й antwoord van ≈Й vraag doodtrek (kanselleer) en nie oordoen nie, merk die 
doodgetrekte (gekanselleerde) poging.  
 
вАҐ Volgehoue akkuraatheid (CA) word in ALLE aspekte van die nasienriglyn toegepas, maar dit 
hou by die tweede berekeningsfout op.  
 
вАҐ Wanneer ≈Й kandidaat aflees van ≈Й grafiek, tabel, uitlegplan en kaart en ekstra antwoorde gee, 
penaliseer vir elke ekstra item.  
  
(EC/ NOVEMBER  2023) MATHEMATICAL LITERACY P2  3

KEY TO TOPIC SYMBOL:  
F = Finance; M  = Measurement; MP = Maps, plans and other representations ; P= Probability

Symbol  Explanation  
M  Method  
M/A  Method with accuracy  
MCA  Method with consistent accuracy  
CA Consistent accuracy  
A Accuracy  
C Conversion  
S Simplification  
RT/RG/RM  Reading from a table OR Reading from a graph OR Read from a map 
F Choosing the correct formula  
SF Substitution in a formula  
J Justification  
P Penalty, e.g.  for no units, incorrect rounding off etc.  
R Rounding off OR Reason  
AO Answer only  
NPR  No penalty for rounding

 Symbol  Explanation  
M  Method  
MA  Method with accuracy  
CA  Consistent accuracy  
MCA  Method with consistent accuracy  
A  Accuracy  
C  Conversion  
S  Simplification  
RT/RG/RM  Reading from a table/Reading from a graph/Read from  a map 
F  Choosing the correct formula  
SF  Substitution in a formula  
J  Justification  
P  Penalty, e.g.  for no units, incorrect rounding off etc.  
R  Rounding Off/Reason  
AO Answer only  
NPR  No penalty for rounding

MARKS:  100 
 
Symbol  Explanation  
M  Method  
MA  Method with accuracy  
CA  Consistent accuracy  
A  Accuracy  
C  Conversion  
S  Simplification  
RT/RG/RM  Reading from a table/Reading from a graph/Read from map  
F  Choosing the correct formula  
SF  Substitution in a formula  
J  Justification  
P  Penalty, e.g. for no units, incorrect rounding off etc.  
R  Rounding Off/Reason  
AO Answer only  
NPR  No penalty for rounding

MARKING GUIDELINES   
  
NOTE:   
  
пВЈ If a candidate answers a question TWICE, only mark the FIRST attempt.  
пВЈ If a candidate has crossed out (cancelled) an attempt to a question and NOT redone 
the solution, mark the crossed out (cancelled version)  
пВЈ Consistent accuracy (CA) applies in ALL aspects of th e marking guidelines, 
however it stops at the second calculation error.  
пВЈ If the candidate presents any extra solution when reading from a graph, table, layout 
plan and map, then penalise for every extra incorrect item presented.   
  
LET WEL:   
  
пВЈ As ≈Й kandidaat ≈Й vraag TWEE keer beantwoord, merk slegs die EERSTE poging.  
пВЈ As ≈Й kandidaat ≈Й antwoord van ≈Й vraag doodtrek (kanselleer) en nie oordoen nie, 
merk die doodgetrekte (gekanselleerde) poging.  
пВЈ Volgehoue akkuraatheid (CA) word in ALLE aspekte van die nasienriglyn toegepas, 
maar dit hou by die tweede berekeningsfout op.  
пВЈ Wanneer ≈Й kandidaat aflesings vanaf ≈Й grafiek, tabel, uitlegplan en kaart geneem 
en ekstra antwoorde gee, penaliseer vir elke ekstra verkeerde item.

SYMBOL  EXPLANATION   
A Accuracy   
CA Consistent Accuracy   
C Conversion   
J Justification (Reason/Opinion)   
M Method   
MA Method with accuracy   
P Penalty for no units, incorrect rounding off, etc.   
R Rounding off   
RT/RG  Reading from table/graph   
S Simplification   
SF Correct substitution in a formula   
O Own opinion
